file(GLOB INTERFACES
  "../cppInterface/2.3.2/include/*/*/*.h"
)

add_library(${PROJECT_NAME} SHARED ${SOURCE_LIST} ${SOURCE_LIST_SKIP_UNITY} ${INTERFACES})

source_group(TREE ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/.. FILES ${SOURCE_LIST} ${SOURCE_LIST_SKIP_UNITY} ${INTERFACES})

set_source_files_properties(${SOURCE_LIST_SKIP_UNITY} PROPERTIES SKIP_UNITY_BUILD_INCLUSION true)

target_compile_features(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE cxx_std_11)

set(gcc_cxx "$<COMPILE_LANG_AND_ID:CXX,GNU,Clang>")
set(msvc_cxx "$<COMPILE_LANG_AND_ID:CXX,MSVC>")

if(WIN32)
  if(MSVC_TOOLSET_VERSION EQUAL "143")
    set(compilerVersion "vs2022")
  elseif(MSVC_TOOLSET_VERSION EQUAL "142")
    set(compilerVersion "vs2019")
  elseif(MSVC_TOOLSET_VERSION EQUAL "141")
    set(compilerVersion "vs2017")
  elseif(MSVC_TOOLSET_VERSION EQUAL "140")
    set(compilerVersion "vs2015")
  else()
    set(compilerVersion "UNKNOWN")
  endif()
else()
  if(CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_ID STREQUAL "Clang")
    set(compilerVersion "clang")
  elseif(CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_ID STREQUAL "GNU")
    set(compilerVersion "gcc")
  else()
    set(compilerVersion "UNKNOWN")
  endif()
  string(FIND ${CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_VERSION} "." majorDot)
  string(SUBSTRING ${CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_VERSION} 0 ${majorDot} majorVer)
  string(CONCAT compilerVersion ${compilerVersion} ${majorVer})
  if((CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_VERSION VERSION_LESS 5.0) AND (CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_ID STREQUAL "GNU"))
    MATH(EXPR majorDot "${majorDot}+1")
    string(SUBSTRING ${CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_VERSION} ${majorDot} -1 minorString)
    string(FIND ${minorString} "." minorDot)
    string(SUBSTRING ${minorString} 0 ${minorDot} minorVer)
    string(CONCAT compilerVersion ${compilerVersion} ${minorVer})
  endif()
endif()

if(WIN32)
else()
  if(CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_ID STREQUAL "Clang")
    option(BUILD_ENABLE_ASAN "Enable building the project with address sanitizer compiler flags" OFF)
    option(BUILD_ENABLE_MSAN "Enable building the project with memory sanitizer compiler flags" OFF)
    option(BUILD_ENABLE_TSAN "Enable building the project with thread sanitizer compiler flags" OFF)
    option(BUILD_ENABLE_USAN "Enable building the project with undefined behavior sanitizer compiler flags" OFF)
  endif()
  option(BUILD_USE_OLD_DWARF "Enable building the project with the dwarf-4 flag" OFF)
endif()

target_compile_definitions(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
  "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:UCI_BUILDING_DLL>>"
  "$<${msvc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:UCI_BUILDING_DLL;_UNICODE;_WIN32_WINNT=0x0601;WIN32_LEAN_AND_MEAN;_CRT_SECURE_NO_WARNINGS>>"
)
target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
  "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-Wall;-pedantic;-fvisibility=hidden;-fvisibility-inlines-hidden;-Wno-overloaded-virtual>>"
  "$<${msvc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:/bigobj;/MP;/wd4250;/W3;/EHs>>"
  "$<$<AND:${msvc_cxx},$<VERSION_GREATER_EQUAL:${MSVC_TOOLSET_VERSION},141>>:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:/permissive-;/Zc:__cplusplus>>"
  "$<$<AND:${msvc_cxx},$<VERSION_GREATER_EQUAL:${MSVC_TOOLSET_VERSION},142>>:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:/W4>>"
)
target_link_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
  "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-Wl,--version-script=${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../CALGeneration/calgt/SDK/cal-gt/build/starterKitCAL/CAL.version>>"
  "$<${msvc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:/INCREMENTAL:NO;/LARGEADDRESSAWARE>>"
)
if(CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER_ID STREQUAL "Clang")
  if(BUILD_ENABLE_ASAN)
    target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fsanitize=address;-fno-omit-frame-pointer>>"
    )
    target_link_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fuse-ld=lld;-fsanitize=address>>"
    )
  elseif(BUILD_ENABLE_MSAN)
    target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fsanitize=memory;-fno-omit-frame-pointer>>"
    )
    target_link_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fuse-ld=lld;-fsanitize=memory>>"
    )
  elseif(BUILD_ENABLE_TSAN)
    target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fsanitize=thread>>"
    )
    target_link_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fuse-ld=lld;-fsanitize=thread>>"
    )
  elseif(BUILD_ENABLE_USAN)
    target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fsanitize=undefined>>"
    )
    target_link_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
      "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-fuse-ld=lld;-fsanitize=undefined>>"
    )
  endif()
endif()
if(BUILD_USE_OLD_DWARF)
  target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
    "$<${gcc_cxx}:$<BUILD_INTERFACE:-gdwarf-4>>"
  )
endif()

set(Boost_ROOT ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/boost/dist/boost_1_83_0)
set(Boost_USE_STATIC_LIBS ON)
find_package(Boost 1.76.0 REQUIRED COMPONENTS oms_regex oms_thread oms_chrono oms_random oms_filesystem)
if(Boost_FOUND)
  target_include_directories(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE ${Boost_INCLUDE_DIRS})
  target_link_libraries(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE ${Boost_LIBRARIES})
endif()

target_include_directories(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
  ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/include
  ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../cppInterface/2.3.2/include
)

target_include_directories(${PROJECT_NAME} SYSTEM PRIVATE
  "$<${gcc_cxx}:${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/activemq-cpp/dist/activemq-cpp-library-3.9.5/${compilerVersion}/include/activemq-cpp-3.9.5>"
  "$<${gcc_cxx}:${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/apache_apr/dist/apr-1.7.4/${compilerVersion}/include/apr-1>"
  "$<${msvc_cxx}:${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/activemq-cpp/dist/activemq-cpp-library-3.9.5/${compilerVersion}/include/activemq-cpp-3.9.5>"
  "$<${msvc_cxx}:${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/apache_apr/dist/apr-1.7.4/${compilerVersion}/include/apr-1>"
)

if(WIN32)
  target_link_libraries(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
    debug ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/activemq-cpp/dist/activemq-cpp-library-3.9.5/${compilerVersion}/lib/Debug/activemq-cpp.lib
    debug ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/apache_apr/dist/apr-1.7.4/${compilerVersion}/lib/Debug/apr-1.lib
    optimized ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/activemq-cpp/dist/activemq-cpp-library-3.9.5/${compilerVersion}/lib/Release/activemq-cpp.lib
    optimized ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/apache_apr/dist/apr-1.7.4/${compilerVersion}/lib/Release/apr-1.lib
    Mswsock Rpcrt4 WS2_32
  )
else()
  target_link_libraries(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
    ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/activemq-cpp/dist/activemq-cpp-library-3.9.5/${compilerVersion}/lib/libactivemq-cpp.a
    ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/../../../../COTS/apache_apr/dist/apr-1.7.4/${compilerVersion}/lib/libapr-1.a
    ${CMAKE_DL_LIBS}
  )
endif()

if(WIN32)
  install (TARGETS ${PROJECT_NAME} DESTINATION ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/lib/${compilerVersion}_${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}_$<CONFIG>)
  install (FILES $<TARGET_PDB_FILE:${PROJECT_NAME}> DESTINATION ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/lib/${compilerVersion}_${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}_$<CONFIG> OPTIONAL)
else()
  install (TARGETS ${PROJECT_NAME} DESTINATION ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/lib/${compilerVersion}_$<CONFIG>)
endif()
